layout: "post"
title: "The circle"
date: "2018-05-01"
agda: true
toc: true
categories: type-theory
---

In this entry, we want to show some equivalences
between the circle and other higher inductive types.

{% comment %}

{: . equation }

  $$\sum\,{\mathbb{S}^1}\,(\mathsf{rec}_{\mathbb{S}^1}\, \mathcal{U}\,  2\,
  (\mathsf{ua}(\mathsf{rec}_{2}2 1_{2} 0_{2}))) \simeq \mathbb{S}^1.$$

I gave a talk giving one solution using the flattening lemma:

- [**Direct link PDF**](https://github.com/jonaprieto/flattenlem/files/2045561/Jonathan-Prieto-Cubides-The-Flattening-Lemma.pdf)

{% endcomment %}

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="616" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="621" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="628" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">2018-07-06-mini-hott</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

##  S¹ type

The circle is the higher inductive type with one point
and one no trivial path called path as we show in the following
picture.

![path](/assets/ipe-images/circle.png)
*Figure 1. The circle type `S¹`.*

## `pS` type

![path](/assets/ipe-images/tour-type.png)
*Figure 2. `pS` Type.*

## Equivalences

### Lemma 1

{: .equation }

  $$ \mathsf{S}^{1} \simeq \mathsf{pS}. $$

**Proof**.

Let us define the outgoing functions:

<a id="3989" class="Keyword">private</a>

The proof of the homotopy $$ f' ∘ g' \sim \mathsf{id}$$.

Finally,

### Lemma 3

{: .equation}
  $$
    \Sigma~S^{1}~P~\simeq~pS
  $$

  where $$P (\mathsf{base}) :≡ \mathsf{Bool}$$ and $$\mathsf{ap~P~loop~=~ua~(neg)}$$.

          <a id="14069" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13162" class="Function">d̰</a>
         <a id="14081" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#8018" class="Function Operator">∎</a>

<a id="14084" class="Comment">-- ΣSP-≃-pS : Σ S¹ P ≃ pS</a>
<a id="14110" class="Comment">-- ΣSP-≃-pS = qinv-≃ f {!   !}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14168" class="Comment">-- -- Defs.</a>
<a id="14180" class="Comment">--     γ₀₁   = transport-ua P loop neg-eq (S¹-βrec Type₀ Bool (ua neg-eq)) false</a>
<a id="14261" class="Comment">--     g-p₀₁ = pair= (loop , γ₀₁)</a>
<a id="14295" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="14298" class="Comment">--     γ₁₀   = transport-ua P loop neg-eq (S¹-βrec Type₀ Bool (ua neg-eq)) true</a>
<a id="14378" class="Comment">--     g-p₁₀ = pair= (loop , γ₁₀)</a>
<a id="14412" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="14415" class="Comment">--     g : pS → Σ S¹ P</a>
<a id="14438" class="Comment">--     g = -- 0   ↦ (base, 0)</a>
<a id="14468" class="Comment">--         -- 1   ↦ (base, 1)</a>
<a id="14498" class="Comment">--         -- p₀₁ ↦ (base, 0) == (base, 1)</a>
<a id="14541" class="Comment">--         -- p₁₀ ↦ (base, 1) == (base, 0)</a>
<a id="14584" class="Comment">--         pS-rec</a>
<a id="14602" class="Comment">--             (Σ S¹ P)</a>
<a id="14626" class="Comment">--             (base , false)</a>
<a id="14656" class="Comment">--             (base , true)</a>
<a id="14685" class="Comment">--             g-p₀₁</a>
<a id="14706" class="Comment">--             g-p₁₀</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14752" class="Comment">-- -- Missing lemmas.</a>
<a id="14774" class="Comment">--     postulate</a>
<a id="14791" class="Comment">--       lemma-ap-f-γ₀₁ : ap f (pair= (loop , γ₀₁)) == p₀₁</a>
<a id="14850" class="Comment">--       lemma-ap-f-γ₁₀ : ap f (pair= (loop , γ₁₀)) == p₁₀</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Let us prove the homotopies:
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14963" class="Comment">-- Homotopy</a>
    <a id="14979" class="Comment">-- f-g : f ∘ g ∼ id</a>
    <a id="15003" class="Comment">-- f-g = pS-ind (λ ps → (f ∘ g) ps == id ps) q₀ q₁ dpath₁ dpath₂</a>
    <a id="15072" class="Comment">--   where</a>
    <a id="15087" class="Comment">--</a>
    <a id="15094" class="Comment">--     q₀ : (f ∘ g) pS₀ == id pS₀</a>
    <a id="15132" class="Comment">--     q₀ = p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15152" class="Comment">--</a>
    <a id="15159" class="Comment">--     q₁ : (f ∘ g) pS₁ == id pS₁</a>
    <a id="15197" class="Comment">--     q₁ = p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15217" class="Comment">--</a>
    <a id="15224" class="Comment">--     dpath₁ :  q₀ == q₁ [ (λ z → (f ∘ g) z == id z) ↓ p₀₁ ]</a>
    <a id="15290" class="Comment">--     dpath₁ =</a>
    <a id="15310" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
    <a id="15329" class="Comment">--         transport (λ z → (f ∘ g) z == id z) p₀₁ q₀</a>
    <a id="15387" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ transport-eq-fun (f ∘ g) id p₀₁ q₀ ⟩</a>
    <a id="15445" class="Comment">--         ! ap (f ∘ g) p₀₁ · q₀ · ap id p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15494" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (! ap (f ∘ g) p₀₁ · q₀ ·_) (ap-id p₀₁) ⟩</a>
    <a id="15559" class="Comment">--         ! ap (f ∘ g) p₀₁ · q₀ · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15602" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! r · q₀ · p₀₁) (! ap-comp g f p₀₁) ⟩</a>
    <a id="15671" class="Comment">--         ! ap f (ap g p₀₁) · q₀ · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15715" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! ap f r · q₀ · p₀₁)</a>
    <a id="15767" class="Comment">--                  (pS-βrec₀₁ ((Σ S¹ (λ b → P b))) (base , false) (base , true) g-p₀₁ g-p₁₀) ⟩</a>
    <a id="15867" class="Comment">--         ! ap f g-p₀₁ · q₀ · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="15906" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! r · q₀ · p₀₁) lemma-ap-f-γ₀₁ ⟩</a>
    <a id="15970" class="Comment">--         ! p₁₀ · q₀ · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="16002" class="Comment">--           ==⟨⟩</a>
    <a id="16024" class="Comment">--         ! p₁₀ · p₁₀ · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="16057" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (_· p₀₁) (·-linv p₁₀) ⟩</a>
    <a id="16105" class="Comment">--         idp · p₀₁</a>
    <a id="16130" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ·-lunit p₀₁ ⟩</a>
    <a id="16165" class="Comment">--         q₁</a>
    <a id="16183" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
    <a id="16198" class="Comment">--</a>
    <a id="16205" class="Comment">--     dpath₂ : q₁ == q₀ [ (λ z → (f ∘ g) z == id z) ↓ p₁₀ ]</a>
    <a id="16270" class="Comment">--     dpath₂ =</a>
    <a id="16290" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
    <a id="16309" class="Comment">--         transport (λ z → (f ∘ g) z == id z) p₁₀ q₁</a>
    <a id="16367" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ transport-eq-fun (f ∘ g) id p₁₀ q₁ ⟩</a>
    <a id="16425" class="Comment">--         ! ap (f ∘ g) p₁₀ · q₁ · ap id p₁₀</a>
    <a id="16474" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (! ap (f ∘ g) p₁₀ · q₁ ·_) (ap-id p₁₀) ⟩</a>
    <a id="16539" class="Comment">--         ! ap (f ∘ g) p₁₀ · q₁ · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="16582" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! r · q₁ · p₁₀) (! ap-comp g f p₁₀) ⟩</a>
    <a id="16651" class="Comment">--         ! ap f (ap g p₁₀) · q₁ · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="16695" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! ap f r · q₁ · p₁₀)</a>
    <a id="16747" class="Comment">--                  (pS-βrec₁₀ ((Σ S¹ (λ b → P b))) (base , false) (base , true) g-p₀₁ g-p₁₀) ⟩</a>
    <a id="16847" class="Comment">--         ! ap f g-p₁₀ · q₁ · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="16886" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (λ r → ! r · q₁ · p₁₀) lemma-ap-f-γ₁₀ ⟩</a>
    <a id="16950" class="Comment">--         ! p₀₁ · q₁ · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="16982" class="Comment">--           ==⟨⟩</a>
    <a id="17004" class="Comment">--         ! p₀₁ · p₀₁ · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="17037" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ap (_· p₁₀) (·-linv p₀₁) ⟩</a>
    <a id="17085" class="Comment">--         idp · p₁₀</a>
    <a id="17110" class="Comment">--           ==⟨ ·-lunit p₁₀ ⟩</a>
    <a id="17145" class="Comment">--         q₀</a>
    <a id="17163" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17199" class="Comment">-- -- Homotopy</a>
<a id="17214" class="Comment">--     g-f : g ∘ f ∼ id</a>
<a id="17238" class="Comment">--     g-f (s , pₛ) = g-f&#39; s pₛ</a>
<a id="17270" class="Comment">--       where</a>
<a id="17285" class="Comment">--         g-f&#39; : (s : S¹) → (pₛ : P s) → (g ∘ f) (s , pₛ) == id (s , pₛ)</a>
<a id="17359" class="Comment">--         g-f&#39; = S¹-ind (λ s → (pₛ : P s) → (g ∘ f) (s , pₛ) == id (s , pₛ)) qb qpath</a>
<a id="17446" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="17449" class="Comment">--           where</a>
<a id="17468" class="Comment">--           qb : (pₛ₁ : P base) → (g ∘ f) (base , pₛ₁) == id (base , pₛ₁)</a>
<a id="17543" class="Comment">--           qb true  = g-p₀₁</a>
<a id="17573" class="Comment">--           qb false = g-p₁₀</a>
<a id="17603" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="17606" class="Comment">--           qpath : qb == qb [(λ z → (pₛ₁ : P z) → (g ∘ f) (z , pₛ₁) == id (z , pₛ₁)) ↓ loop ]</a>
<a id="17702" class="Comment">--           qpath =</a>

<a id="17835" class="Comment">--                 ==⟨ {!   !}  ⟩</a>
<a id="17869" class="Comment">--               qb</a>
<a id="17889" class="Comment">--             ∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
